For people listening to him the first time :  He is ex member of Berywam (the ones who rocked AGT stage twice)  Berywam name comprises of 4 beatboxers ( you can search them on youtube ) they all are french champions Be : Beatness Ry : Rhythmind Wa : wawad M : Mb14 (replaced by the new guy now)  Mb14 is in this video, but he has served in berywam for over 10 years. They won many international beatbox championships together. But mb14 wasn't getting the fame he needed so he left for a solo journey.  You can follow more at swissbeatbox and beatbox international youtube channels. And BeatboxBattleTV for every 4 year world champs.

Ill preface this with saying, yes hes good at what he does, BUT, what hes doing isnt actually beatboxing. Beatboxing at its core is using no equipment to help. Hes using a sound board to reverberate and replay his sounds, thats not what beatboxing is. You look up any professional beatboxer and youll see them making all this same sound while using nothing but a microphone and nothing else. So yes while hes good at what he does, its not exactly beatboxing. Again, you can just go watch pretty much any other beatboxer and see they use absolutely no other equipment.

This is something anyone can do by using a vocal synthesizer.  A vocal synthesizer just means that we are using the human voice as the instrument that is being synthesized.   The human voice is already the perfect instrument, but a synthesizer can change the function of the human voice and the instrument itself.
